Prompt: 'What are the risks of having high blood pressure?\n' 
Generated text: '\nThe risk of heart disease is 2 to 6 times greater if you have high blood pressure, compared to people with normal blood pressure.\n\nHigh blood pressure is usually caused by an imbalance in the amount of salt in the blood (sodium). When the kidneys excrete salt, some of it stays in the body to act as a buffer against the loss of sodium and fluids (water) from the body. If this buffer is depleted, it can cause high blood pressure.\n\nWhat causes high blood pressure?\n\nHigh blood pressure is the result of a build up of pressure in the arteries and veins. This is caused by a number of factors. These include:\n\nFamily history\n\nAged 65 years and over\n\nObesity\n\nFasting glucose\n\nSmoking\n\nAlcohol consumption\n\nCardiovascular disease is a major cause of mortality, especially in older people. The following are some risk factors for cardiovascular disease:\n\nFamily history\n\nAged 65 years and over\n\nObesity\n\nDiabetes mellitus\n\nAged 45 years and over\n\nSmoking\n\nAlcohol consumption\n\nHigh blood pressure is usually inherited. However, some people develop high blood pressure from other risk factors, such as smoking.\n\nWhat are the symptoms of high blood pressure?\n\nSymptoms of high blood pressure can include:\n\nFrequent urination\n\nDizziness\n\nDry mouth\n\nHeartburn\n\nChest pain\n\nFeeling light-headed, faint or a fast heartbeat\n\nRestlessness\n\nNausea\n\nBlurred vision\n\nWhat are the treatment options for high blood pressure?\n\nThere is no cure for high blood pressure, but your doctor may be able to reduce the risk of complications by treating your high blood pressure.\n\nThere are three main treatment options for high blood pressure:\n\nDietary treatment (also known as ‘lifestyle’)\n\nBlood pressure medication\n\nHypertensive disorder\n\nHigh blood pressure is most commonly treated with lifestyle changes. These include:\n\nCutting down on salt\n\nExercising at least 150 minutes per week\n\nEating a healthy balanced diet\n\nIn most cases, this type of treatment is suitable for most people.\n\nIn some cases, your doctor may recommend blood pressure medication to treat high blood pressure. Some blood pressure medications are available without a prescription'

Prompt: 'What lifestyle changes can help prevent and lower high blood pressure?\n' 
Generated text: "Here are some lifestyle changes you can make to help prevent high blood pressure:\n1. Eat less salt.\nThe Institute of Medicine recommends a maximum of 2,300 milligrams of sodium a day, or less than two teaspoons.\n2. Cut back on processed foods.\nThat includes hot dogs, soups, breakfast cereals, chips, crackers, and ready-to-eat foods.\n3. Get moving.\nTry to get 150 minutes of moderate-intensity activity a week, or 75 minutes of vigorous activity.\n4. Do less stress.\nThat includes managing your workload and setting limits on how many hours you spend in front of the TV.\n5. Cut back on alcohol.\nHave no more than one drink a day for women and two for men.\n6. Quit smoking.\nIt's a proven fact that smoking increases the risk of high blood pressure."

Prompt: 'What kind of medicines can help control high blood pressure?\n' 
Generated text: '\nA:\n\nQuick Answer\n\nSome common medicines to help control high blood pressure include diuretics, beta-blockers and calcium channel blockers, according to WebMD. Some of these drugs are combined with a diuretic in a pill called a diuretic-beta blocker combination pill, while others are combined with a calcium channel blocker in a pill called a calcium channel blocker-beta blocker combination pill.\n\nKeep Learning\n\nDiuretics reduce the amount of water in the body, causing it to lose sodium and become more concentrated, notes the Mayo Clinic. Beta-blockers reduce the heart rate, which allows the heart to work more efficiently and reduces the amount of oxygen the heart has to use. Calcium channel blockers help relax the blood vessels, allowing more blood to move through them, according to WebMD.'

Prompt: 'What is the difference between bronchiolitis and bronchitis?\n' 
Generated text: '\nA:\n\nQuick Answer\n\nThere is no difference between bronchiolitis and bronchitis; however, bronchiolitis is the more serious of the two conditions. Bronchiolitis is inflammation of the airways of the lungs, according to Medline Plus.\n\nKeep Learning\n\nBronchiolitis is more common than bronchitis and can be a serious, life-threatening condition. Bronchiolitis is caused by viruses and bacteria, and it can be spread from person to person. Bronchiolitis can be caused by the seasonal flu virus and the respiratory syncytial virus, according to Medline Plus.\n\nBronchitis is a more mild respiratory condition than bronchiolitis. Bronchitis is inflammation of the bronchi, which are the airways that connect the lungs to the airways of the throat and mouth. Bronchitis can be caused by a virus or a bacterial infection, according to Medline Plus.'

The primary goal of treatment for high blood pressure is to reduce the force of the blood against the walls of the arteries, preventing the hardening of the arteries, reducing the risk of heart disease, and preventing blood from leaking into the spaces between the heart and the lungs. Treatment options for high blood pressure include lifestyle changes, blood pressure medications, and when necessary, a combination of both.\n\nLifestyle changes\n\nLifestyle changes are a primary way of lowering blood pressure. Health professionals encourage individuals to make changes to their diet, regular exercise, and weight. They also encourage individuals to drink enough water, limit alcohol, and avoid smoking. In addition, health professionals encourage individuals to follow a healthy sleep schedule. People who have high blood pressure should avoid sleeping for 12 hours or more a day.\n\nBlood pressure medications\n\nDoctors may prescribe blood pressure medications to individuals with high blood pressure. Prompt: 'What are the possible causes of laryngitis?\n' 
Generated text: '\nLaryngitis is an inflammation of the larynx, the voice box, which can cause coughing, difficulty breathing, and other symptoms. The inflammation can be caused by bacteria, viruses, or fungi. The most common causes are bacteria (Streptococcus pneumoniae, Staphylococcus aureus) and viruses (Human parainfluenza virus type 1, Respiratory syncytial virus). The common types of fungi (Candida species) may also be associated with laryngitis.\n\nTreatment\n\nTreatment options depend on the cause of the laryngitis and the type of bacteria, virus, or fungus involved. Treatment usually consists of rest and taking an antibiotic medication called an aminoglycoside. This is an antibiotic that is given by mouth. Taking the medication may help prevent a secondary infection of the larynx.\n\nRevision Information\n\nThis content is reviewed regularly and is updated when new and relevant evidence is made available. This information is neither intended nor implied to be a substitute for professional medical advice. Always seek the advice of your physician or other qualified health provider prior to starting any new treatment or with questions regarding a medical condition.'
